While the shoulder rig and the snubby revolver holster is GREAT, the accompanying speedloader pouch is WAY to LARGE for the 5 round speedloaders.  They will actually hold 6 round speedloaders loosely.  The problem with this is that a small frame person (who will be using this concealment rig) will have an obvious bulge on the speedloader side (forcing your arm and elbow away form your body.  This rig is useless for me/us, until I can either find a smaller speedloader pouch, or a loose ammo pouch that can be mounted on the off side of this rig.  $155 spent that we can not use yet...< /review>

<user_id>100383433465617435879</user_id><user_name>J D< /user_name><Date>1598893117077<//Date><Rating>3</Rating>< review>
The order was processed and product shipped in a timely manner.  The holster I received from Aker appears to be of high quality.  However, it is an EXTREMELY tight fit on my Smith & Wesson 329PD .44 Magnum revolver.  The holster is intended for Smith & Wesson N-Frame revolvers, which the 329PD is, but it is very difficult to get my revolver out of the holster once the gun is holstered in place.  I expect this extremely tight fit may possibly relax with time.  However, the much more significant problem is that the thumb strap is way, way too short to actually wrap around the hammer of the revolver and snap together.  The thumb strap is approximately 1-inch too short.  It is not even close to being able to snap together with the revolver holstered.  I am making efforts to try to stretch the thumb strap, but, given the high quality of the leather that the holster is constructed from, I am not certain I will be able to stretch the thumb strap enough to make it work.</review>

Generally quite good. Glock 23 very tight fit when holster arrived. Literally five hundred-plus insertions to loosen, and several  over-nights with pistol wrapped in plastic bag in holster. Still tight, but since I'm not into fast-draw competition, the draw is acceptable. Also a very comfortable fit, and much more concealable than any IWB I've used, need for cover garment notwithstanding. Would appreciate two improvements in design: (1)Would be good to have the option of belt tie downs, especially on the pistol side, and (2) as a left hander, I would like to see the mag pouches angles reversed, allowing a single, smooth drop into hand, ready to insert into pistol without having to spin the mag first.
But, again, overall a good and relatively timely service and would probably rate it at 4 Â½.  As I heard many times in my forty years as a union carpenter, "Close enough for Government Work".< /review>

<Text>I ordered a Boba tea. The drink itself was good, but the tapioca pearls were disappointingly bland. They lacked any sort of sweetness whatsoever. My guess is that they were stored in plain water rather than a sugar syrup like most Boba places would use. That could be a simple improvement to implement.

Also, just glancing at the yogurt toppings on display, the various candy coated m&m type toppings were white and chalky like they were either old or weren't stored properly. It didn't look particularly appetizing. Seems penny-wise but pound-foolish for a yogurt shop to have stale toppings on display like that.</Text></record></dataset><record>

< text>
Not only do they serve frozen yogurt, but they also have sandwiches and shave ice!

There were six flavors of froyo when I dropped in:

* Vanilla - How can you go wrong with this one?
* Blood orange (non-dairy) - Couldn't really taste the blood orange part...
* Red velvet - Good, but not a big fan of red velvet froyo
* Banana - Don't like it, didn't try it!
* Pina colada - My favorite, more coconut than pina colada
* Chocolate - Also good.

Love the painted Hawaiian mural on the wall. The servings are gigantic too! A small will cost $3, but is large enough to share for two. Easily.< /text>

< Review>
I had a two for one issue with both my heating and air conditioning unit going out. Being in inland San Diego this was an issue as it gets cold during the night and blistering hot during the day. I didn't want just any yokel contractor working on it because I hate having people come back three times for the same issue.

I checked these guys reviews after doing a search and they seemed to be very legit. The day of the appointment I sat waiting for the inevitable 10 to 15 minutes late appointment. To my surprise they actually showed up a minute early.

After shaking hands I led them to air conditioning unit to let them work their blue collar magic bracing myself for a huge repair bill since the furnace and ac were out.

After all was said and done it did cost me (not that going with someone else would have made much difference) But I have to say they fixed everything promptly and I haven't needed to call their techs back for any reason.

That's a reason for a top rating in my book.</Review>
